narrative_event = {
	id = wikid.1
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.1
	title = "EVTTITLEwikid.1" #Old man and a Map
	picture = GFX_evt_monk
	
	ai = no
	only_playable = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	min_age = 16
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		has_ambition = obj_obtain_valyrian_sword
		start_date = 7886.1.1 #post doom only
		is_nomadic = no
		OR = {
			is_female = no
			female_get_masculine_event_trigger = yes
			trait = ambitious	
			trait = proud
			trait = authoritative
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = someone_doing_valyrian_sword }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = obj_valyrian_sword } 
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_quest_started } 
			had_character_flag = { flag = wikid_quest_started days = 3650 }
		}
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		NOT = { trait = kingsguard }
		NOT = { trait = nightswatch }	
		in_command = no
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 180

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			wealth = 250
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			wealth = 500
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			wealth = 1000
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.1" # Let's hear what he has to say.
		trigger = { has_ambition = obj_obtain_valyrian_sword }
		hidden_tooltip = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.2 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.1" # Kick him out of my castle!
		trigger = { has_ambition = obj_obtain_valyrian_sword }
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "You are a cheating scumbag."  # Death IRL
		trigger = { NOT = { has_ambition = obj_obtain_valyrian_sword } }
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = wikid.3
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.3 #Old man says go here bring a companion
	#title = "EVTTITLEwikid.3" #The Plan - old man tells lord he is certain about (can mention any location as will be shipwrecked @unknown later for greg type lore qq)
	picture = "GFX_evt_spymaster"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.3" # I am ready and prepared to undertake this 
		narrative_event = { id = wikid.4 days = 1 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.4 }
		clr_character_flag = wikid_quest_started 
		set_character_flag = wikid_quest_started	
		set_global_flag = someone_doing_valyrian_sword
		if = { #recent doom valyria
			limit = { 
				start_date = 7886.1.1
				NOT = { year = 7950 } 
			}
			set_character_flag = wikid_quest_claim_valyria	
		}
		wealth = -100
		any_artifact = { #just in case they inherited a wikid artifact from another quester
			limit = { has_artifact_flag = wikid_quest_artifact }
			clr_artifact_flag = wikid_quest_artifact
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.3" # I am not ready
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = wikid.4
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.4 #you think and choose
	title = "EVTTITLEwikid.4" #The Fellowship of House [ROOT.GetOnlyDynastyName]
	picture = GFX_tutors

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		narrative_event = { id = wikid.5 days = 7 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.4" #  Bring me a great warrior		
		capital_scope = {
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = { ai = no }
					create_random_soldier = {
						random_traits = yes
						dynasty = NONE
						female = no

						culture = PREV
						name = Фашбиндер
						trait = brave
						trait = strong	
						historical = yes
					}
				}	
				if = {
					limit = { ai = yes }
					create_random_soldier = {
						random_traits = yes
						dynasty = NONE
						female = no
						religion = ROOT
						culture = PREV
						trait = brave
						trait = strong	
						historical = yes
					}
				}
				new_character = {
					random_list = {
						10 = { add_trait = trained_warrior }
						33 = { add_trait = skilled_warrior }
						10 = { add_trait = master_warrior }
					}
					random = {
						chance = 25
						add_trait = quick
					}
					set_character_flag = fash_can_be_inbred
					character_event = { id = wikid.499 }
					if = {
						limit = { religion = the_seven }
						knight_character_effect = yes
					}				
				}
			}	
		}		
		set_character_flag = wikid_warrior
	}

			}

character_event = { #give companion random parent to avoid culling
	id = wikid.499

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid.326_new_man } }
			set_character_flag = wikid_companion
		}
		remove_trait = imbecile
		remove_trait = inbred
		remove_trait = slow
		remove_trait = infirm
		remove_trait = incapable
		remove_trait = leper
		remove_trait = possessed
		remove_trait = ill
		remove_trait = pneumonic
		remove_trait = maimed
		remove_trait = crippled
		remove_trait = content
		set_immune_to_pruning = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = fash_can_be_inbred }
			random_list = {
				1 = { add_trait = inbred }
				99 = { }
			}
			clr_character_flag = fash_can_be_inbred
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

character_event = {

	desc = EVTDESCwikid.6 # you leave
	title = "EVTTITLEwikid.6" #The Departed
	picture = GFX_evt_trade_post_republic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
		narrative_event = { id = wikid.7 days = 30 random = 30 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.6" #  You leave
		add_trait = wikid
		set_character_flag = do_not_disturb

			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			add_trait = wikid
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
			set_character_flag = do_not_disturb
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.51 days = 1000 } }#fail safe
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = wikid.8
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.8
	picture = GFX_evt_monk
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.8" #  HAPPY TIMES
		from = { character_event = { id = wikid.9 days = 2 } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = lustful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = hedonist
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { has_fair_trait_trigger = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = chaste
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = celibate
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				personal_opinion = { who = FROM value = 10 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				personal_opinion = { who = FROM value = 25 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				personal_opinion = { who = FROM value = 40 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				personal_opinion = { who = FROM value = 55 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FROM = { has_character_modifier = wol_seducer_1 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.25
				FROM = { has_character_modifier = wol_seducer_2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5.0
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						trait = seducer
						trait = seductress
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.8" #  Pls no
		from = { character_event = { id = wikid.10 days = 2 } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
				
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { has_ugly_trait_trigger = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { personal_opinion = { who = FROM value = -10 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { personal_opinion = { who = FROM value = -25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { personal_opinion = { who = FROM value = -40 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { personal_opinion = { who = FROM value = -55 } }
			}
		}
	}
}	

#You went into froms cabin and got success
character_event = {
	id = wikid.9
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.9
	picture = GFX_sansa
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.9" #  Yay
		FROM = {
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_wikid_quest_like multiplier = 2 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = { trait = stressed }
			remove_trait = stressed
		}	
		if = {
			limit = { trait = depressed }
			remove_trait = depressed
		}	
		if = {
			limit = { trait = wounded }
			remove_trait = wounded
		}	
		#remove_trait = maimed ##yeah kinda op but this quest chain uses wound/maim as death chance factors.
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { #pirates
					trigger = { NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_quest_claim_valyria } }

		}

character_event = {
	id = wikid.12
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.12
	picture = GFX_evt_battle
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTZwikid.12" #  WIN CYVASSE evtoptZ
		trigger = { has_character_flag = wikid_cyvasse_3 }
		character_event = { id = wikid.16 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.12" #  Attack Dragon with Archer
		if = {  #good choice
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_cyvasse_2 }
			set_character_flag = wikid_cyvasse_3
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_cyvasse_1 }
			set_character_flag = wikid_cyvasse_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = { not = { has_character_flag = wikid_cyvasse_1 } }
			set_character_flag = wikid_cyvasse_1
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_courtier = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
				character_event = { id = wikid.11 }
			}	
		}
	}

		if = {  #bad choice
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_cyvasselose_2 }
			set_character_flag = wikid_cyvasselose_3
		}
		if = {  
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_cyvasselose_1 }
			set_character_flag = wikid_cyvasselose_2
		}
		if = {  
			limit = { not = { has_character_flag = wikid_cyvasselose_1 } }

#I have beaten my companion FROMFROM
character_event = {
	id = wikid.181
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.181
	picture = GFX_trial_by_combat
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	show_from_from = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.181" #  End Quest
		trigger = { FROMFROM = { is_alive = no } }
		narrative_event = { id = wikid.51 days = 30 random = 15 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.51 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.181" #  Practice makes Perfect
		trigger = { FROMFROM = { is_alive = yes } }
		set_character_flag = wikid_won_companion_duel
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_wikid_quest_like }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { #pirates
					trigger = { NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_quest_claim_valyria } }
					narrative_event = { id = wikid.20 days = 50 random = 25 } 
				}
				50 = { #new tangent
					narrative_event = { id = wikid.80 days = 50 random = 25 }
				}
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = skilled_warrior }
			random = {
				chance = 10
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = trait_notification.21 } }
				tooltip = { add_trait = master_warrior }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = trained_warrior }
			random = {
				chance = 20
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = trait_notification.21 } }
				tooltip = { add_trait = skilled_warrior }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOR = {
					trait = trained_warrior 
					trait = skilled_warrior
					trait = master_warrior
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { remove_trait = poor_warrior }
			add_trait = trained_warrior
		}
	}	
}
#Duel was a draw
character_event = {
	id = wikid.182
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.182
	picture = GFX_trial_by_combat
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	show_from_from = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.181" #  Practice makes Perfect
		set_character_flag = wikid_won_companion_duel
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { #pirates
					trigger = { NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_quest_claim_valyria } }
					narrative_event = { id = wikid.20 days = 50 random = 25 } 
				}
				50 = { #new tangent
					narrative_event = { id = wikid.80 days = 50 random = 25 }
				}
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = trained_warrior }
			random = {
				chance = 10
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = trait_notification.21 } }
				tooltip = { add_trait = skilled_warrior }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				trait = poor_warrior
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = trait_notification.21 } }
				tooltip = { add_trait = trained_warrior }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				NOR = {
					trait = poor_warrior 
					trait = trained_warrior 
					trait = skilled_warrior
					trait = master_warrior
				}
			}
			add_trait = poor_warrior
		}
	}	
}

#A fight with the pirates!
character_event = {
	id = wikid.26
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.26
	picture = GFX_knights
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
		random_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {				
				trait = pirate
				prisoner = no
				war = no
				combat_rating = 20
				age = 16
				NOT = { has_severe_disability_trigger = yes }
				ai = yes
			}
			set_character_flag = wikid_pirate1
			save_event_target_as = wikid_pirate1
			break = yes
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {				
				trait = pirate
				prisoner = no
				war = no
				combat_rating = 20
				age = 16
				NOT = { has_severe_disability_trigger = yes }
				is_female = no
				ai = yes
				liege = { ai = yes }
			}
			set_character_flag = wikid_pirate1
			save_event_target_as = wikid_pirate1
			break = yes
		}
		e_rebels = { 
			holder_scope = {	
				create_random_soldier = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = NONE
					female = no
					religion = pirate
					culture = lysene
					#name = "Капитан Спэк Джерроу"
					trait = pirate
				}
				new_character = {
					remove_trait = inbred
					remove_trait = imbecile
					remove_trait = infirm
					remove_trait = incapable
					remove_trait = dwarf
					remove_trait = hunchback
					remove_trait = clubfooted
					remove_trait = weak
					remove_trait = leper
					remove_trait = possessed
					remove_trait = ill
					remove_trait = pneumonic
					remove_trait = maimed
					random_list = {
						30 = { add_trait = poor_warrior }
						30 = { add_trait = trained_warrior }
						30 = { add_trait = skilled_warrior }
						10 = { add_trait = master_warrior }
					}
					add_trait = one_eyed #cool pirates!!
					save_event_target_as = wikid_pirate1
					set_character_flag = wikid_pirate1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.26" # I will fight
		set_character_flag = wikid_player_vs_pirate
		set_character_flag = flag_duel_to_the_death
		event_target:wikid_pirate1 = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_suprize_attacked_pirates } 
				}
				add_trait_silently_wounded_effect = yes
			}
			character_event = { id = wikid.27 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.27 } 
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.26" # My companion will fight
		event_target:wikid_pirate1 = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_suprize_attacked_pirates } 
				}
				add_trait_silently_wounded_effect = yes
			}
			character_event = { id = wikid.27 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.27B } 
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = wikid.30
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.30
	picture = GFX_knights
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.30" #but alas [fromfrom.getSheHe] died.
		trigger = { 
			FROM = { has_character_flag = wikid_pirate1 }
		}
		set_character_flag = wikid_dead_companion
		set_character_flag = wikid_player_vs_pirate
		FROM = { character_event = { id = wikid.27 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.27 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.30" #[from.getSheHe] won!
		trigger = { 
			FROM = { 
				has_character_flag = wikid_companion 
				NOT = { trait = wounded }
				NOT = { is_maimed_trigger = yes }
			}			
		}
		set_character_flag = wikid_companion_duel_won
		hidden_tooltip = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.32 } }
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_wikid_quest_like }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.30" #[from.getSheHe] won but was wounded
		trigger = { 
			FROM = { 
				has_character_flag = wikid_companion 
				trait = wounded
			}			
		}
		set_character_flag = wikid_companion_duel_won_wounded
		hidden_tooltip = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.32 } }
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_wikid_quest_dislike }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTCwikid.30" #[from.getSheHe] won but was maimed
		trigger = { 
			FROM = { 
				has_character_flag = wikid_companion 
				is_maimed_trigger = yes
			}			
		}
		set_character_flag = wikid_companion_duel_won_maimed
		hidden_tooltip = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.32 } }
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_wikid_quest_dislike multiplier = 2 }
		}
	}
}

narrative_event = {
	id = wikid.33
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.33
	title = "EVTTITLEwikid.33"

	picture = GFX_evt_merchant_ship_at_sea_republic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.33" 
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_flag_ship_taken }
			random_artifact = {
				limit = { 
					has_artifact_flag = flagship 
					is_artifact_equipped = yes
				}
				destroy_artifact = yes			
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = wikid_dead_companion
				}
				random_list = {
					100 = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.60 days = 30 } 
					}
					#0 = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.XXXXXXXX days = 30 } 
					#}
					#0 = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.XXXXXXXX days = 30 } 
					#}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_dead_companion }
				}
				random_list = {
					50 = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.64 days = 30 } 
					}
					50 = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.70 days = 30 } 
					}
					#0 = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.XXXXXXXXXXXX days = 30 } 
					#}
				}
			}
		}	
	}
}

	}
}

character_event = {
	id = wikid.361
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.361 # Citadel makes things pretty
	picture = GFX_evt_monk
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	hide_from = yes
	
	trigger = { FROM = { is_alive = yes } }

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.361" #Correct
		trigger = { 
			FROM = {
				#OPTION 1
				has_character_flag = wikid_mural_direwolf
				has_character_flag = wikid_mural_eagle
				has_character_flag = wikid_mural_crow
				OR = {
					and = {
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler1_pos1 #eagle
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler2_pos2 #crow
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler3_pos4 #wolf
					}
					and = {
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler2_pos1 #eagle
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler1_pos2 #crow
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler3_pos4 #wolf
					}
					and = {
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler2_pos1 #eagle
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler3_pos2 #crow
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler1_pos4 #wolf
					}
					and = {
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler1_pos1 #eagle
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler3_pos2 #crow
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler2_pos4 #wolf
					}
					and = {
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler3_pos1 #eagle
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler2_pos2 #crow
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler1_pos4 #wolf
					}

						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler2_pos2 #crow
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler3_pos3 #dog
					}
					and = {
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler2_pos1 #eagle
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler1_pos2 #crow
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler3_pos3 #dog

						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler2_pos1 #eagle
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler3_pos2 #crow
						has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler1_pos3 #dog

character_event = {
	id = wikid.36
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.36 # Tumbler Result
	#title = "EVTTITLEwikid.36" 
	picture = GFX_pillar_lever
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	trigger = { is_alive = yes }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_courtier = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
				save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.36" #Correct
		trigger = { has_character_flag = wikid_tumble_correct }	
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = { #if companion is dead, proceed straight to ending
				limit = { NOT = { event_target:wikid_companion = { is_alive = yes } } }
				narrative_event = { id = wikid.50 }
			}
			else = {
				narrative_event = { id = wikid.37 }
			}
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.36" #incorrect
		trigger = { NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_tumble_correct } }	
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler_mad }
			if = { 
				limit = { trait = stressed }	
				if = { 
					limit = { trait = depressed }	
					if = { 
						limit = { trait = possessed }	
						if = { 
							limit = { trait = blinded }	
							if = { 
								limit = { trait = lunatic }	
								random_courtier = {
									limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
									add_trait = has_missing
									death = { death_reason = death_suicide }	
								}
								clr_global_flag = someone_doing_valyrian_sword
								add_trait = has_missing
								death = { death_reason = death_suicide }								
							}
							if = { 
								limit = { NOT = { trait = lunatic } }
								add_trait = lunatic	
							}
						}
						if = { 
							limit = { NOT = { trait = blinded } }
							add_trait = blinded	
						}
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { NOT = { trait = possessed } }
						add_trait = possessed	
					}
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { NOT = { trait = depressed } }
					add_trait = depressed	
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { NOT = { trait = stressed } }
				add_trait = stressed		
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler_mad }
			}
			set_character_flag = wikid_tumbler_mad		
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = wikid.35 }	
		}	
	}
}


#Betrayal
narrative_event = {
	id = wikid.37
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.37 # Your companion if alive speaks to you. Treasure chest in the room.
	title = "EVTTITLEwikid.37" #The Betrayal

	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.37" 
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = TOOLTIPwikidCOMPANIONTALK
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = wikid_warrior
					}
					character_event = { id = wikid.40 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = wikid_oldman
					}
					character_event = { id = wikid.41 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = wikid_sailor
					}
					character_event = { id = wikid.42 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = wikid_whore
					}
					character_event = { id = wikid.38 }
				}
			}
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.37" #duel intro
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = TOOLTIPwikidCOMPANIONDUEL
			hidden_tooltip = {
				random_courtier = {
					limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
					set_character_flag = wikid_betrayal_companion
					character_event = { id = wikid.45 }			
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#The Companion - The whore
character_event = {
	id = wikid.38
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.38 # I remember the night we spent together./n/nShe continues;

	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.38"  #It was magical!
		trigger = { 
			has_character_flag = wikid_whore
			has_character_flag = wikid_won_companion_seduce
		}	
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			add_lover = ROOT
			tooltip = { show_portrait = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { same_sex = ROOT }
					fertility = 0.4
					ROOT = { fertility = 0.4 }
					is_pregnant = no
				}	
				if = {
					limit = { is_female = yes }
					impregnate_cuckoo = ROOT
				}	
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_female = no 
						ROOT = { is_pregnant = no }
					}
					ROOT = { impregnate_cuckoo = PREV }
				}
			}	
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.43 } }
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIPwikidcompanionloves }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.38" #I cant believe you did that, I was an untouched maiden.
		trigger = { 
			has_character_flag = wikid_whore
			NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_won_companion_seduce }
			NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_read_book }
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			tooltip = { show_portrait = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { same_sex = ROOT }
					fertility = 0.4
					ROOT = { fertility = 0.4 }
					is_pregnant = no
				}	
				if = {
					limit = { is_female = yes }
					impregnate_cuckoo = ROOT
				}	
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_female = no 
						ROOT = { is_pregnant = no }
					}
					ROOT = { impregnate_cuckoo = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.43 } }
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIPwikidcompanionhates }
	}

#The Companion - Decision
character_event = {
	id = wikid.45
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.45 # 

	picture = GFX_evt_monk
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.45" #YOU'RE A DICK LETS FIGHT!
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_character_flag = dragon_betrayal_decision }
			}	
			set_character_flag = wikid_betrayal_companion
			set_character_flag = flag_duel_to_the_death
			FROM = { 
				set_character_flag = wikid_betrayal_player 
				character_event = { id = wikid.46 }
			}
		}	
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_character_flag = dragon_betrayal_decision
			}	
			FROM = { 
				set_character_flag = companion_betrayal
			}
			clr_character_flag = dragon_betrayal_decision
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_betrayal_companion }#You ignored
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 0 }
				NOR = {
					trait = ruthless
					trait = deceitful
					trait = greedy
					trait = ambitious
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -9 } }
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -19 } }
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -29 } }
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -39 } }
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -49 } }
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -59 } }
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -69 } }
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -79 } }
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -89 } }
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -99 } }
			}

				factor = 1.5
				trait = ruthless

				factor = 1.5
				trait = arbitrary
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = envious
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.45" #YOU'RE A GOOD FELLOW
		if = { #Dragon lair ending
			limit = { 
				has_character_flag = dragon_betrayal_decision
			}	
			clr_character_flag = dragon_betrayal_decision
			break = yes
		}
		if = { #labyrinth ending
			limit = { 
				FROM = { has_character_flag = wikid_labyrinth_ending }
			}	
			FROM = { 
				narrative_event = { id = wikid.120 } 
			}
			break = yes
		}
		#original ending
		FROM = { 
			narrative_event = { id = wikid.48 } 
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50		
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_flag = wikid_betrayal_companion #You ignored
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 9 }
			}		
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 19 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 29 }
			}
			modifier = {

				opinion = { who = FROM value = 39 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 49 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 59 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 69 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 79 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 89 }

#The Companion - Inform Player Betrayed
character_event = {
	id = wikid.46
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.46 # I will kill you now!
	picture = GFX_evt_lunatic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_labyrinth_ending } }
			random = { #25% chance of recovering house sword
				chance = 25
				if = {
					limit = {
						dynasty = 59
						NOT = { any_character = { has_artifact = ice is_alive = yes } }
					}

##Arrive in Volantis/Astapor/Nearby town

narrative_event = {
	id = wikid.81
	title = "EVTTITLEwikid.81" 
	picture = GFX_evt_busy_trading_dock_republic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Volantis
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.81A
		trigger = {
			capital_scope = {
				NOR = {
					region = world_jade_sea
					region = world_ghiscar
					region = world_slavers_bay
					duchy = { title = d_volantis }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#Astapor
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.81B
		trigger = {
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					region = world_jade_sea
					region = world_ghiscar
					region = world_slavers_bay
				}
				NOT = { duchy = { title = d_astapor } }
			}
		}
	}
	#generic
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.81C
		trigger = {
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					duchy = { title = d_astapor }
					duchy = { title = d_volantis }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.81" #Fight!
		character_event = { id = wikid.82 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.82 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.81" #have them murdered
		trigger = { intrigue = 10 }
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		character_event = { id = wikid.83 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.83 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTCwikid.81" #witty retort
		trigger = { diplomacy = 10 }
		tooltip_info = diplomacy
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_wikid_quest_like }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.85 days = 5 } } #leave port
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTDwikid.81" #Ha!
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_wikid_quest_dislike }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.85 days = 5 } } #leave port
	}
}
character_event = { #Fight
	id = wikid.82
	picture = GFX_evt_family_feud_republic
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.82
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.82"
		random_list = {
			70 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.66
					NOT = { combat_rating = 40 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					combat_rating = 60
				}
				prestige = 25
			}
			25 = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { trait = wounded } 
						NOT = { is_maimed_trigger = yes } 
					}
					add_trait_silently_wounded_effect = yes
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 38280 } }
				}
			}
			5 = {
				clr_global_flag = someone_doing_valyrian_sword
				random_friend = {
					limit = { trait = dragon }
					random = {
						chance = 50
						death = { death_reason = death_missing }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { any_artifact = { has_artifact_flag = valyrian_steel } }
					set_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPwikidswordlost }
				}
				any_artifact = {
					limit = { has_artifact_flag = wikid_quest_artifact }
					unsafe_destroy_artifact = yes
				}
				death = { death_reason = death_missing }
				random_courtier = {
					limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
					death = { death_reason = death_missing }
				}				
			}
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_wikid_quest_like }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.85 days = 5 } } #leave port
	}
}

##Feast with local noble
narrative_event = {
	id = wikid.84
	title = "EVTTITLEwikid.84" 
	picture = GFX_evt_busy_trading_dock_republic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Volantis
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.84A
		trigger = {
			capital_scope = {
				NOR = {
					region = world_jade_sea
					region = world_ghiscar
					region = world_slavers_bay
					duchy = { title = d_volantis }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#Astapor
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.84B
		trigger = {
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					region = world_jade_sea
					region = world_ghiscar
					region = world_slavers_bay
				}
				NOT = { duchy = { title = d_astapor } }
			}
		}
	}
	#generic
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.84C
		trigger = {
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					duchy = { title = d_astapor }
					duchy = { title = d_volantis }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.85 days = 5 } } #leave port
		if = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						region = world_jade_sea
						region = world_ghiscar
						region = world_slavers_bay
					}
					NOT = { duchy = { title = d_astapor } }
				}
			}
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = { 
					capital_scope = { duchy = { title = d_astapor } } 
					NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
				}
				save_event_target_as = wikid_feast_host
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = {
					NOT = { duchy = { title = d_volantis } }
					NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
				}
			}
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = { capital_scope = { duchy = { title = d_volantis } } }
				save_event_target_as = wikid_feast_host
			}
			break = yes
		}
		random_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				capital_scope = { region = world_slavers_bay } 
				NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
			}
			save_event_target_as = wikid_feast_host
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.84" #The feast went well
		trigger = {
			event_target:wikid_feast_host = {
				opinion = { who = ROOT value = -15 }
			}
			NOT = { diplomacy = 10 }
		}
		prestige = 25
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_wikid_quest_like }
		}
		event_target:wikid_feast_host = {
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_enjoyed_feast months = 60 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.84" #It went badly
		trigger = {
			event_target:wikid_feast_host = {
				NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = -15 } }
			}
			NOT = { diplomacy = 10 }
		}
		prestige = -25
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_wikid_quest_dislike }
		}
		event_target:wikid_feast_host = {
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_dislike months = 60 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTCwikid.84" #diplomacy
		trigger = { diplomacy = 10 }
		tooltip_info = diplomacy
		prestige = 50
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_wikid_quest_like }
		}
		event_target:wikid_feast_host = {
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_enjoyed_feast months = 60 multiplier = 2 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTDwikid.84" #valyrian knowledge
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { culture_group = valyrian }
			OR = {
				has_character_flag = wikid_valyrian 
				trait = linguist
				has_character_modifier = multilingual
			}	
		}
		prestige = 50
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_wikid_quest_like }
		}
		event_target:wikid_feast_host = {
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_enjoyed_feast months = 60 multiplier = 2 }
		}
	}
}

#Kraken defeated
character_event = {
	id = wikid.91
	desc = "EVTDESCwikid.91"
	picture = GFX_evt_kraken

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.91" 
		prestige = 50
		if = {
			limit = { has_nickname = no }
			give_nickname = nick_the_krakenslayer
		}
		random_list = {
			5 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					is_maimed_trigger = yes
				}
				add_maimed_trait_effect = yes
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = raid_events.28 } } 
			}
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					is_maimed_trigger = yes
				}

			}

				factor = 0.5
				is_weak_trigger = yes
			}
		}

		set_character_flag = valyrian_quest_dragon

			limit = { has_character_flag = valyria_dragon }
			character_event = { id = dragon.2799 tooltip = TOOLTIPdragon.2799 }
			clr_character_flag = valyria_dragon
		}
	}

		name = "EVTOPTCwikid.101" # companion betrays
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = companion_betrayal 
			trait = wikid
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			dragon = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = valyria_dragon }
				tooltip = { show_portrait = yes }
				hidden_tooltip = { add_friend = PREV }
			}
		}	
		character_event = { id = wikid.105 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.105 }
	}

	}

	immediate = {
		random = { #25% chance of recovering house sword
			chance = 25
			set_character_flag = find_dynastic_sword
		}
	}

				NOT = { has_house_words_trigger = yes }
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = "EVTOPTGETHOUSEWORDS"
			trigger = {
				has_house_words_trigger = yes
			}
		}

				has_character_flag = wikid_whore

			}

				add_lover = ROOT
				tooltip = { show_portrait = yes }

					limit = { 
						NOT = { same_sex = ROOT }
						fertility = 0.4
						ROOT = { fertility = 0.4 }
						is_pregnant = no
					}	
					if = {
						limit = { is_female = yes }
						impregnate_cuckoo = ROOT
					}	
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_female = no 
							ROOT = { is_pregnant = no }
						}
						ROOT = { impregnate_cuckoo = PREV }
					}
				}	
			}
		}
		wealth = 500
		narrative_event = { id = wikid.51 days = 60 random = 30 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.51 } #quest ends
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = find_dynastic_sword }

		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.104" 
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				death = { death_reason = death_missing }
			}
		}	
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			death = { death_reason = death_missing }
		}
		random_friend = {
			limit = { trait = dragon }
			death = { death_reason = death_missing }
		}
		clr_global_flag = someone_doing_valyrian_sword	
		hidden_tooltip = { add_trait = fed_to_dragon }
		if = {
			limit = { any_artifact = { has_artifact_flag = valyrian_steel } }
			set_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
			custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPwikidswordlost }
		}
		any_artifact = {
			limit = { has_artifact_flag = wikid_quest_artifact }
			unsafe_destroy_artifact = yes
		}
		death = { 
			death_reason = death_missing
			killer = FROMFROM
		}
	}
}

			custom_tooltip = {
				text = TOOLTIPRENAMEARTIFACTADVICE
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = find_dynastic_sword
	}
	option = {
		name = "You are a cheating scumbag." 
		trigger = { not = { trait = wikid } }
	}
}

##The Labyrinth
#Path 1
character_event = { 
	id = wikid.110
	picture = GFX_dark_corridor	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.110START
		trigger = { 
			has_character_flag = wikid_labyrinth_start 
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.110
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_labyrinth_start }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
		#If somehow AI is doing this, randomly resolve based on learning
		if = {
			limit = { ai = yes }
			random_list = {
				75 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.66
						NOT = { learning = 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.66
						NOT = { learning = 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						learning = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						learning = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						learning = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						learning = 17
					}
					#character_event = { id = wikid. days = 10 }
				}
				20 = {
					random_courtier = {
						limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
						death = { death_reason = death_missing }
					}
					random_friend = {
						limit = { trait = dragon }
						random = {
							chance = 50
							death = { death_reason = death_missing }
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { any_artifact = { has_artifact_flag = valyrian_steel } }
						set_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
						custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPwikidswordlost }
					}
					any_artifact = {
						limit = { has_artifact_flag = wikid_quest_artifact }
						unsafe_destroy_artifact = yes
					}
					death = { death_reason = death_missing }
					clr_global_flag = someone_doing_valyrian_sword	
				}
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_labyrinth }
			}
			set_character_flag = wikid_labyrinth
			set_character_flag = wikid_labyrinth_start
			#6 stages, choice of four pathways, randomise correct pathway at the start for re-playability
			random_list = {
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_1_A }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_1_B }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_1_C }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_1_D }
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_2_A }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_2_B }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_2_C }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_2_D }
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_3_A }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_3_B }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_3_C }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_3_D }
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_4_A }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_4_B }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_4_C }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_4_D }
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_5_A }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_5_B }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_5_C }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_5_D }
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_6_A }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_6_B }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_6_C }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_6_D }
			}
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.110"
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = TOOLTIPwikidLABYRINTHA
			hidden_tooltip = {
				clr_character_flag = wikid_labyrinth_start
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_path_1_A } }
					character_event = { id = wikid.111 days = 1 } #WRONG
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_path_1_A }
					character_event = { id = wikid.112 days = 1 } #CORRECT
				}
			}
		}		
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.110"
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = TOOLTIPwikidLABYRINTHB
			hidden_tooltip = {
				clr_character_flag = wikid_labyrinth_start
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_path_1_B } }
					character_event = { id = wikid.111 days = 1 } #WRONG
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_path_1_B }
					character_event = { id = wikid.112 days = 1 } #CORRECT
				}
			}
		}		
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTCwikid.110"
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = TOOLTIPwikidLABYRINTHC
			hidden_tooltip = {
				clr_character_flag = wikid_labyrinth_start
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_path_1_C } }
					character_event = { id = wikid.111 days = 1 } #WRONG
				}
				if = {

#Incorrect path
character_event = { 
	id = wikid.111
	picture = GFX_dark_corridor	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.111A
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.111B
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.111C
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.111D
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.111E
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
		#Five chances before chance of death	
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_1 } }
			set_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_1
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_1
				NOT = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_2 }
			}
			set_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_2
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_2
				NOT = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_3 }
			}
			set_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_3
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_3
				NOT = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_4 }
			}
			set_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_4
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_4
				NOT = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_5 }
			}
			set_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_5
			break = yes
		}
		set_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_death
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.111"
		trigger = { NOT = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_death } }	
		random_list = {
			88 = { #safely return to start
				character_event = { id = wikid.110 days = 1 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.110 }
			}
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						trait = wounded
						is_maimed_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				add_trait_silently_wounded_effect = yes
				hidden_tooltip = { 
					character_event = { id = 38280 } 
					character_event = { id = wikid.110 days = 1 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.110 }
				}
			}
			2 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					is_maimed_trigger = yes
				}
				add_maimed_trait_effect = yes
				hidden_tooltip = { 
					character_event = { id = wikid.110 days = 1 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.110 }
				}
			}
		}		
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.111"
		trigger = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_death } 
		random_list = {
			70 = { #safely return to start
				character_event = { id = wikid.110 days = 1 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.110 }
			}
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						trait = wounded
						is_maimed_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				add_trait_silently_wounded_effect = yes
				hidden_tooltip = { 
					character_event = { id = 38280 } 
					character_event = { id = wikid.110 days = 1 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.110 }
				}
			}
			5 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					is_maimed_trigger = yes
				}
				add_maimed_trait_effect = yes
				hidden_tooltip = { 
					character_event = { id = wikid.110 days = 1 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.110 }
				}
			}
			5 = {
				random_courtier = {
					limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
					death = { death_reason = death_missing }
				}
				random_friend = {
					limit = { trait = dragon }
					random = {
						chance = 50
						death = { death_reason = death_missing }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { any_artifact = { has_artifact_flag = valyrian_steel } }
					set_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPwikidswordlost }
				}
				any_artifact = {
					limit = { has_artifact_flag = wikid_quest_artifact }
					unsafe_destroy_artifact = yes
				}
				death = { death_reason = death_missing }
				clr_global_flag = someone_doing_valyrian_sword	
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_death		
	}
}

		}

			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {

#Start the adventure!
character_event = {
	id = wikid.2510
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = foreign_adventure
		add_trait = wikid
		set_character_flag = do_not_disturb
		if = {
			limit = { is_councillor = yes }
			remove_title = job_castellan
			#remove_title = title_hand_of_the_king
			#remove_title = title_hand_of_the_emperor
			remove_title = job_chancellor
			remove_title = job_marshal
			remove_title = job_treasurer
			remove_title = job_spymaster
			remove_title = job_physician
			remove_title = job_spiritual
		}
		character_event = { id = wikid.252 days = 800 random = 400 }
		character_event = { id = wikid.9290 days = 1500 } #end quest failsafe
		#character_event = { id = wikid.252 days = 1 }
		if = { #Chance of proposing foreign marriage
			limit = { 
				can_marry_trigger = yes
				NOT = { trait = bastard }
				is_female = no
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				modifier = {
					factor = 4
					has_ambition = obj_get_married
				}
				character_event = { id = wikid.274 days = 299 random = 100 }
			}
		}
		#Chance of finding foreign lover
		random = {
			chance = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = lustful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				has_ambition = obj_find_lover
			}					
			character_event = { id = wikid.280 days = 299 random = 100 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}	
#Adventure outcome selector
character_event = {
	id = wikid.252
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		trait = wikid 
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = do_not_disturb
		if = { #add to seclusion if neccessary
			limit = {
				is_ruler = no
				prisoner = no
				liege = { has_character_modifier = in_seclusion }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = in_seclusion
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = { #Check adventure can end
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = incapable
					prisoner = yes
					is_ruler = yes
				}
			}
			remove_trait = wikid
			clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure
			break = yes
		}
		if = { #Lifestyle?
			limit = {
				learning = 12
				NOT = { lifestyle_traits = 1 }
			}
			random_list = {
				60 = { }
				10 = { set_character_flag = cartographer }
				20 = { set_character_flag = traveller }
				10 = { set_character_flag = linguist }
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			5 = { # Becomes wealthy via trade
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = { stewardship = 10 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					stewardship = 14
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					stewardship = 18
				}
				liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.253 } }
			}
			5 = { # Stranded
				liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.254 } }
			}
			5 = { # Marries foreign peasant
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						is_married = yes
						is_female = yes
						trait = celibate
						trait = eunuch
						trait = proud
						trait = ruthless
					}						
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = humble
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = honorable
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.2
					culture = eastern_valyrian
				}
				liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.256 } }
			}
			10 = { # Stays abroad
				liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.257 } }
			}
			5 = { # Changes Religion
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					trait = zealous		
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					is_devil_worshiper_trigger = yes	
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = cynical
				}
				liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.259 } }
			}
			10 = { # Improves Personality
				liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.260 } }
			}
			10 = { # Improves Diplomacy
				liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.261 } }
			}
			10 = { # Improves Intrigue
				liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.262 } }
			}
			5 = { # Captured by Pirates!
				liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.263 } }
			}
			5 = { # Injured
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							trait = rude
							trait = proud
							trait = wroth
							trait = cruel
						}
					}	
				}
				liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.265 } }
			}
			5 = { # Reaches Nefer
				modifier = { #Only highly competent people can do this
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						NOT = { stewardship = 10 }
						NOT = { diplomacy = 10 }
						NOT = { martial = 10 }
					}	
				}
				modifier = { #Only these regions
					factor = 0
					liege = {
						capital_scope = { 
							NOT = { region = world_westeros }
							NOT = { region = world_summer_sea }
							NOT = { region = world_ghiscar }
						}	
					}					
				}
				liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.266 } }
			}
			5 = { # Reaches Asshai
				modifier = { #Only highly competent people can do this
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						NOT = { stewardship = 10 }
						NOT = { diplomacy = 10 }
						NOT = { martial = 10 }
					}	
				}
				modifier = { #Only these regions
					factor = 0
					liege = {
						capital_scope = { 
							NOT = { region = world_westeros }
						}	
					}					
				}
				liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.268 } }
			}
			5 = { # Reaches Oldtown
				modifier = { #Only highly competent people can do this
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						NOT = { stewardship = 10 }
						NOT = { diplomacy = 10 }
						NOT = { martial = 10 }
					}	
				}
				modifier = { #Only these regions
					factor = 0
					liege = {
						capital_scope = {
							NOT = { region = world_far_east }
						}	
					}					
				}
				liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.270 } }
			}
			5 = { # Reaches far to the south
				modifier = { #Only highly competent people can do this
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						NOT = { stewardship = 10 }
						NOT = { diplomacy = 10 }

					}	
				}
				modifier = { #NOT these regions
					factor = 0
					liege = {
						capital_scope = {
							region = world_summer_sea
						}	
					}					
				}
				liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.272 } }
			}
			5 = { # Becomes party animal/hedonist
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						trait = shy
						trait = chaste
						trait = celibate
						trait = temperate
						trait = hedonist
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = drunkard
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = gregarious
				}
				modifier = {

				}

					factor = 0

# Becomes wealthy via trade
character_event = {
	id = wikid.253
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.253
	picture = GFX_evt_merchant_ship_at_sea_republic
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = { #select random foreign realm for event text
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					demesne_size = 1
					NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
					higher_tier_than = DUKE
					is_nomadic = no
					NOT = { trait = wildling }
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
					NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
				}
				save_event_target_as = foreign_realm
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			random_list = {
				10 = { set_character_flag = trade_200 }
				10 = { set_character_flag = trade_300 }
				10 = { set_character_flag = trade_400 }
				10 = { set_character_flag = trade_500 }
				10 = { set_character_flag = trade_750 }
			}
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.253	
		event_target:foreign_realm = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } }
		FROM = {
			remove_trait = wikid
			clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = trade_200 }
				prestige = 100
				wealth = 200
				clr_character_flag = trade_200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = trade_300 }
				prestige = 150
				wealth = 300
				clr_character_flag = trade_300
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = trade_400 }
				prestige = 200
				wealth = 400
				clr_character_flag = trade_400
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = trade_500 }
				prestige = 250
				wealth = 500
				clr_character_flag = trade_500
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = trade_750 }
				prestige = 375
				wealth = 750
				clr_character_flag = trade_750
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_funded_trip } }
				wealth = -100
				ROOT = { wealth = 100 }
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = cartographer }
				add_trait = cartographer
				clr_character_flag = cartographer
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = traveller }
				add_trait = traveller
				clr_character_flag = traveller
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = linguist }
				add_trait = linguist
				clr_character_flag = linguist
			}
			add_character_modifier = { 
				name = went_on_foreign_tour
				duration = -1
			}			
		}
		clear_event_target = foreign_realm
	}
}
# Stranded
character_event = {
	id = wikid.254
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.254
	picture = GFX_evt_desert
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		#select random foreign realm for event text
		random_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				demesne_size = 1
				NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
				higher_tier_than = DUKE
				is_nomadic = no
				NOT = { trait = wildling }
				is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
				NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
			}
			save_event_target_as = foreign_realm
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.254 #send rescue
		event_target:foreign_realm = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } }
		wealth = -100
		FROM = { 
			remove_trait = wikid
			clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure	
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = rescued_my_sorry_ass
				multiplier = 0.5
			}			
			clr_character_flag = cartographer
			clr_character_flag = traveller
			clr_character_flag = linguist
		}
		clear_event_target = foreign_realm
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBwikid.254 #No
		prestige = -50
		FROM = { 
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_angry
				months = 36
			}
			random_list = {
				35 = {
					
				}	
				20 = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { trait = stressed } }
						add_trait = stressed
					}	
				}
				20 = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_ill = no }
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									has_dlc = "Reapers"
								}
							}
							add_trait = ill
							hidden_tooltip = {
								character_event = {
									id = 38290
								}
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_dlc = "Reapers"
							}
							add_symptom_effect = yes
						}	
					}
				}
				15 = {
					imprison = event_target:foreign_realm
					event_target:foreign_realm = {
						hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.255 } }
					}	
				}
				10 = {
					random_friend = {
						limit = { trait = dragon }
						random = {
							chance = 50
							death = { death_reason = death_missing }
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { any_artifact = { has_artifact_flag = valyrian_steel } }
						set_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
						custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPwikidswordlost }
					}
					any_artifact = {
						limit = { has_artifact_flag = wikid_quest_artifact }
						unsafe_destroy_artifact = yes
					}
					death = { death_reason = death_missing }
				}
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_alive = yes }
				remove_trait = wikid
				clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure	
			}
			clr_character_flag = cartographer
			clr_character_flag = traveller
			clr_character_flag = linguist
		}
		clear_event_target = foreign_realm
	}
}

# Stays abroad
character_event = {
	id = wikid.257
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.257
	picture = GFX_evt_recieve_letter
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		#select random foreign realm for event text
		random_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				demesne_size = 1
				NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
				higher_tier_than = DUKE
				is_nomadic = no
				NOT = { trait = wildling }
				is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
				NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
			}
			save_event_target_as = foreign_realm
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.257
		event_target:foreign_realm = {
			tooltip = { show_portrait = yes }
			FROM = { 
				move_character = PREV 
				remove_trait = wikid
				clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure
				prestige = 150
				if = {
					limit = { has_character_flag = cartographer }
					add_trait = cartographer
					clr_character_flag = cartographer
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_character_flag = traveller }
					add_trait = traveller
					clr_character_flag = traveller
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_character_flag = linguist }
					add_trait = linguist
					clr_character_flag = linguist
				}
				add_character_modifier = { 
					name = went_on_foreign_tour
					duration = -1
				}	
				any_spouse = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						is_ruler = no
						liege = { character = ROOT }
					}
					move_character = PREVPREV
					any_child = {
						limit = {
							is_adult = no
							is_ruler = no
							liege = { character = ROOT }
							is_child_of = PREVPREV	
						}
						move_character = PREVPREVPREV
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character_modifier = in_seclusion
						liege = { NOT = { has_character_modifier = in_seclusion } }
					}
					remove_character_modifier = in_seclusion
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.258 } }
		}
		clear_event_target = foreign_realm
	}
}

	}
	picture = { 
		trigger = { 
			FROM = { is_female = no }
		} 
		picture = GFX_evt_son_asking_father
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

		if = { #select random foreign realm for event text
			limit = { ai = no }

				limit = {

					NOT = { trait = wildling }

					NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
					NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }

			}
		}
		FROM = {
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						trait = humble
					}

				}

				}

				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {

					}

				}

					set_character_flag = rude
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = { trait = selfish }
					}
					set_character_flag = selfish
				}
			}
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.260
		event_target:foreign_realm = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } }
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = humble }
				if = {
					limit = { trait = proud }
					remove_trait = proud
				}
				add_trait = humble
				clr_character_flag = humble
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = diligent }
				if = {
					limit = { trait = slothful }
					remove_trait = slothful
				}
				add_trait = diligent
				clr_character_flag = diligent
			}

				limit = { has_character_flag = kind }

				clr_character_flag = kind
			}

				limit = { has_character_flag = charitable }
				if = {
					limit = { trait = greedy }
					remove_trait = greedy
				}
				add_trait = charitable
				clr_character_flag = charitable
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = patient }
				if = {
					limit = { trait = wroth }
					remove_trait = wroth
				}
				add_trait = patient
				clr_character_flag = patient
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = brave }
				if = {
					limit = { trait = craven }
					remove_trait = craven
				}
				add_trait = brave
				clr_character_flag = brave
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = gregarious }
				if = {
					limit = { trait = shy }
					remove_trait = shy
				}
				add_trait = gregarious
				clr_character_flag = gregarious
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = just }
				if = {
					limit = { trait = arbitrary }
					remove_trait = arbitrary
				}
				add_trait = just
				clr_character_flag = just
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = rude }
				remove_trait = rude
				clr_character_flag = rude
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = selfish }
				remove_trait = selfish
				clr_character_flag = selfish
			}
			remove_trait = wikid
			clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure
			prestige = 150

				limit = { has_character_flag = cartographer }
				add_trait = cartographer
				clr_character_flag = cartographer
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = traveller }
				add_trait = traveller
				clr_character_flag = traveller
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = linguist }
				add_trait = linguist
				clr_character_flag = linguist
			}
			add_character_modifier = { 
				name = went_on_foreign_tour
				duration = -1
			}				
		}
		clear_event_target = foreign_realm
	}
}

# Captured by Pirates!
character_event = {
	id = wikid.263
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.263
	picture = GFX_evt_reaving_ship_lost
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		#select random foreign realm for event text
		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					demesne_size = 1
					NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
					higher_tier_than = DUKE
					is_nomadic = no
					NOT = { trait = wildling }
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
					NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
				}
				save_event_target_as = foreign_realm
			}
		}	
		#select random pirate
		random_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				demesne_size = 1
				NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
				higher_tier_than = BARON
				is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
				trait = pirate
			}
			save_event_target_as = pirate
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.263
		event_target:foreign_realm = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } }
		event_target:pirate = {
			tooltip = { show_portrait = yes }
			FROM = { 
				imprison = PREV 
				remove_trait = wikid
				clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure
				clr_character_flag = cartographer
				clr_character_flag = traveller
				clr_character_flag = linguist
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.264 } }
		}
		clear_event_target = foreign_realm
		clear_event_target = pirate
	}
}

# Injured
character_event = {
	id = wikid.265
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.265
	picture = GFX_evt_torture
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = { #select random foreign realm for event text
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					demesne_size = 1
					NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
					higher_tier_than = DUKE
					is_nomadic = no
					NOT = { trait = wildling }
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
					NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
				}
				save_event_target_as = foreign_realm
			}
		}	
		FROM = {
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						trait = blinded
					}
					set_character_flag = blinded
				}
				10 = { 
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						trait = eunuch
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						is_female = yes
					}
					set_character_flag = eunuch
				}
				10 = { 
					set_character_flag = tortured
				}
				10 = { 
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						trait = disfigured_AGOT
					}
					set_character_flag = disfigured
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { trait = brave }
					NOT = { trait = craven }
					NOT = { trait = berserker }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					set_character_flag = craven
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.265
		event_target:foreign_realm = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } }
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = blinded }
				add_trait = blinded
				clr_character_flag = blinded
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = eunuch }
				add_trait = eunuch
				clr_character_flag = eunuch
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = tortured }
				add_character_modifier = { 
					name = tortured
					duration = 365
				}
				clr_character_flag = tortured
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = disfigured }
				add_trait = disfigured_AGOT
				clr_character_flag = disfigured
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_character_flag = craven
				}
				add_trait = craven
			}
			remove_trait = wikid
			clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure
			add_character_modifier = { 
				name = went_on_foreign_tour
				duration = -1
			}	
			clr_character_flag = cartographer
			clr_character_flag = traveller
			clr_character_flag = linguist
		}
		clear_event_target = foreign_realm
	}
}

long_character_event = {
	id = wikid.266
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.266
	picture = GFX_evt_merchant_ship_at_sea_republic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		#select random foreign realm for event text
		random_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				demesne_size = 1
				NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
				higher_tier_than = DUKE
				is_nomadic = no
				NOT = { trait = wildling }
				is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
				NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
			}
			save_event_target_as = foreign_realm
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.266
		event_target:foreign_realm = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } }
		FROM = {
			remove_trait = wikid
			clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure
			prestige = 500
			wealth = 500
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = cartographer }
				add_trait = cartographer
				clr_character_flag = cartographer
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = traveller }
				add_trait = traveller
				clr_character_flag = traveller
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = linguist }
				add_trait = linguist
				clr_character_flag = linguist
			}
			add_character_modifier = { 
				name = went_on_foreign_tour
				duration = -1
			}	
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = { 
					ai = no
					OR = {
						same_realm = ROOT
						religion_group = ROOT
						dynasty = FROM
					}
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
				}
				character_event = { id = wikid.267 }
			}
		}
	}
}

###Mid Quest Events###
# Proposes foreign marriage
character_event = {
	id = wikid.274
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		can_marry_trigger = yes
		NOT = { trait = bastard }
		trait = wikid
		has_character_flag = foreign_adventure
		prisoner = no
		NOT = { trait = incapable }
		has_epidemic = no
		liege = {
			is_close_relative = ROOT
			dynasty = ROOT
			higher_tier_than = COUNT
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_playable_ruler = { #find random marriage target
			limit = {
				demesne_size = 1
				NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
				ROOT = { 
					liege = { 
						NOT = { lower_tier_than = PREVPREV } 
						is_within_diplo_range = PREVPREV
					} 
				}
				OR = {
					is_patrician = yes
					higher_tier_than = COUNT
				}
				is_nomadic = no
				NOT = { trait = wildling }
				NOT = { trait = pirate }
				is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
				NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
				is_theocracy = no
				any_child = {
					is_alive = yes
					is_female = yes
					is_ruler = no
					liege = { character = PREVPREV }
					age = 12
					NOT = { age_diff = { who = ROOT years = 11 } }
					can_marry_trigger = yes
					prisoner = no
					NOT = { trait = incapable }
					NOT = { trait = bastard }
					has_epidemic = no
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = wikid.275 }
		}
	}
		
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
character_event = {
	id = wikid.275
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.275
	picture = GFX_evt_emissary
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_child = { #find daughter
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
				is_female = yes
				is_ruler = no
				liege = { character = PREVPREV }
				age = 12
				NOT = { age_diff = { who = FROM years = 11 } }
				can_marry_trigger = yes
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { trait = bastard }
				has_epidemic = no
			}
			save_event_target_as = foreign_marriage_daughter
		}
		FROM = { #find out if needs liege permission
			if = {
				limit = {
					liege = { #Is liege's child or grnadchild
						any_child = {
							OR = {
								character = PREVPREV
								any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREV }
							}
						}
					}
				}	
				set_character_flag = needs_liege_permission
			}	
		}
		#Determine marriage prestige
		if = {
			limit = { 
				FROM = { 
					OR = {
						father_even_if_dead = { tier = emperor } 
						mother_even_if_dead = { tier = emperor } 
					}	
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				FROM = { 
					OR = {
						father_even_if_dead = { tier = king } 
						mother_even_if_dead = { tier = king } 
					}	
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				FROM = { 
					OR = {
						father_even_if_dead = { tier = duke } 
						mother_even_if_dead = { tier = duke } 
					}	
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75
			break = yes
		}
		set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35
	}
		
	option = {
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAwikid.275 #Yes, Adventurer is free to choose
			trigger = { 
				FROM = { has_character_flag = needs_liege_permission }
			}
		}	
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTBwikid.275 #Yes, Adventurer needs permission
			trigger = { 
				FROM = { NOT = { has_character_flag = needs_liege_permission } }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			
			modifier = { #No actual alliance to be gained
				factor = 0.33
				FROM = {
					liege = {
						NOT = { sibling = PREV }
						NOT = { is_child_of = PREV }
					}
					NOT = { has_character_flag = needs_liege_permission }
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Would prefer a matrilineal marriage
				factor = 0
				is_patrician = no
				event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = {
					ROOT = { current_heir = { character = PREVPREV } }
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				religion_group = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FROM = { liege = { religion_group = ROOT } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = zealous
