# Acquires foreign lover
character_event = {
	id = wikid.280
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		NOT = { trait = widowed }
		NOT = { trait = eunuch }
		NOT = { trait = celibate }
		NOT = { trait = chaste }
		trait = wikid
		has_character_flag = foreign_adventure
		prisoner = no
		NOT = { trait = incapable }
		has_epidemic = no
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_playable_ruler = { #find random target
			limit = {
				demesne_size = 1
				NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
				higher_tier_than = DUKE
				is_nomadic = no
				NOT = { trait = wildling }
				is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
				NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
				any_courtier = {
					is_alive = yes
					OR = {
						AND = {
							same_sex = ROOT
							trait = homosexual
							ROOT = { trait = homosexual }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { same_sex = ROOT }
							NOT = { trait = homosexual }
							ROOT = { NOT = { trait = homosexual } }
						}
						AND = {
							trait = lustful
							ROOT = { 
								trait = lustful
								culture_group = dornish
							}
						}
					}	
					is_ruler = no
					has_lover = no
					is_close_relative = PREV
					liege = { character = PREVPREV }
					age = 16
					NOT = { age_diff = { who = ROOT years = 11 } }
					prisoner = no
					NOT = { trait = celibate }
					NOT = { trait = incapable }
					NOT = { trait = chaste }				
					opinion = { who = ROOT value = -20 }
					reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -20 }
					has_epidemic = no
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = wikid.281 }
		}
	}
		
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
character_event = {
	id = wikid.281
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.281
	picture = GFX_evt_viking_throneroom_oldgods
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = { #find lover
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
				OR = {
					AND = {
						same_sex = FROM
						trait = homosexual
						FROM = { trait = homosexual }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { same_sex = FROM }
						NOT = { trait = homosexual }
						FROM = { NOT = { trait = homosexual } }
					}
				}
				is_ruler = no
				has_lover = no
				is_close_relative = PREV
				liege = { character = PREVPREV }
				age = 16
				NOT = { age_diff = { who = FROM years = 11 } }
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { trait = celibate }
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { trait = chaste }				
				opinion = { who = FROM value = -20 }
				reverse_opinion = { who = FROM value = -20 }
				has_epidemic = no
			}
			save_event_target_as = foreign_lover
			add_lover = FROM
		}
	}
		
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.281
		event_target:foreign_lover = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } }
		FROM = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_gracious_host
				months = 120
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.282 } } } }
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = wikid.287
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.287
	picture = GFX_evt_feast
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.287
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_ruler = no } }
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { liege = { tier = EMPEROR } } }
				prestige = 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { liege = { tier = KING } } }
				prestige = 15
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { liege = { lower_tier_than = KING } } }
				prestige = 5
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.288 } } } }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_ruler = yes } }
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tier = EMPEROR } }
				prestige = 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tier = KING } }
				prestige = 30
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { lower_tier_than = KING } }
				prestige = 20
			}
		}
	}
}

# Becomes party animal
character_event = {
	id = wikid.289
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.289
	picture = GFX_evt_brothel
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = { #select random foreign realm for event text
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					demesne_size = 1
					NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
					higher_tier_than = DUKE
					is_nomadic = no
					NOT = { trait = wildling }
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
					NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
				}
				save_event_target_as = foreign_realm
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = lustful } }
			random = {
				chance = 33
				set_character_flag = lustful
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = lovers_pox } }
			random = {
				chance = 33
				set_character_flag = minor_disease_herpes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = drunkard } }
			random = {
				chance = 33
				set_character_flag = drunkard
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.289
		FROM = {
			add_trait = hedonist
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = lustful }
				clr_character_flag = lustful
				add_trait = lustful
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = minor_disease_herpes }
				clr_character_flag = minor_disease_herpes
				add_trait = lovers_pox
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = drunkard }
				clr_character_flag = drunkard
				add_trait = drunkard
			}
			remove_trait = wikid
			clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure
			piety = -100
			prestige = 150	
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = cartographer }
				add_trait = cartographer
				clr_character_flag = cartographer
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = traveller }
				add_trait = traveller
				clr_character_flag = traveller
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = linguist }
				add_trait = linguist
				clr_character_flag = linguist
			}
			add_character_modifier = { 
				name = went_on_foreign_tour
				duration = -1
			}				
		}
		clear_event_target = foreign_realm
	}
}
# Finds dragonhorn in smoking sea
long_character_event = {
	id = wikid.2899
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.2899
	picture = GFX_evt_merchant_ship_at_sea_republic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		#select random foreign realm for event text
		random_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				demesne_size = 1
				NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
				higher_tier_than = DUKE
				is_nomadic = no
				NOT = { trait = wildling }
				is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
				NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
			}
			save_event_target_as = foreign_realm
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.2899
		event_target:foreign_realm = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } }
		FROM = {
			remove_trait = wikid
			clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure
			prestige = 500
			wealth = 250
			add_character_modifier = { 
				name = went_on_foreign_tour
				duration = -1
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = cartographer }
				add_trait = cartographer
				clr_character_flag = cartographer
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = traveller }
				add_trait = traveller
				clr_character_flag = traveller
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = linguist }
				add_trait = linguist
				clr_character_flag = linguist
			}
			tooltip = { add_artifact = dragon_horn_a }
			hidden_tooltip = {
				random_list = { #two designs
					1 = { add_artifact = dragon_horn_a }
					1 = { add_artifact = dragon_horn_b }
				}
				new_artifact = { 
					set_artifact_flag = heirloom_@PREV
				} 
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = { 
					ai = no
					OR = {
						same_realm = ROOT
						religion_group = ROOT
						dynasty = FROM
					}
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
				}
				character_event = { id = wikid.2898 }
			}
		}
	}
}

### Player goes on foreign tour
# Decide destination
character_event = {
	id = wikid.295
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.295
	picture = GFX_evt_map
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				ai = no
				OR = {
					trait = traveller
					AND = {
						NOT = { age = 30 }	
						NOT = { trait = content }
						NOT = { trait = slothful }
						NOT = { has_character_modifier = went_on_foreign_tour }	
					}
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = can_foreign_tour
		}
	}
	
	option = { # More
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.295
		trigger = { 
			ai = no
			has_character_flag = can_foreign_tour
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = page_1 }
			clr_character_flag = page_1
			set_character_flag = page_2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = page_2 }
			clr_character_flag = page_2
			set_character_flag = page_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = page_3 }
			clr_character_flag = page_3
			set_character_flag = page_1
		}
		character_event = { id = wikid.295 }
	}
	option = { # Cancel
		name = CANCEL
		trigger = { 
			has_character_flag = page_1
			NOT = { has_character_flag = can_foreign_tour }
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		clr_character_flag = page_1
		clr_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour
	}
	option = { # Make Royal Progress
		name = EVTOPTIwikid.295
		trigger = { 
			has_character_flag = page_1
			higher_tier_than = DUKE
			OR = {
				government = feudal_government
				government = feudal_government_LP
			}
			NOT = { has_character_modifier = made_progress }
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		if = { #optimisation: only trigger full events if a player or any vassal is a player
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					any_player = { is_liege_or_above = ROOT }
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = touring_royal_progress
			character_event = { id = wikid.296 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.296I }
		}	
		else = { #else resolve immediately
			wealth = -100
			add_character_modifier = { name = progress_entourage_large duration = 365 }
			random = { #storm/bandit death chance
				chance = 1
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.2
				}
				if = {
					limit = { any_artifact = { has_artifact_flag = valyrian_steel } }
					set_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPwikidswordlost }
				}
				random_friend = {
					limit = { trait = dragon }
					random = {
						chance = 50
						death = { death_reason = death_missing }
					}
				}
				death = { death_reason = death_missing }
			}
			random = { #wound chance
				chance = 1
				if = { 
					limit = { is_maimed_trigger = yes } 
					health = -1
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { trait = wounded } 
					hidden_tooltip = { remove_trait = wounded }
					add_maimed_trait_effect = yes 
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						NOT = { trait = wounded }
						NOT = { is_maimed_trigger = yes } 
					}
					add_trait_silently_wounded_effect = yes 
				}
			}
			any_realm_lord = { #pick 5 random destinations
				count = 5
				limit = {
					higher_tier_than = BARON
					demesne_size = 1
					NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
					NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
					in_command = no
					war = no 
					prisoner = no		
					has_epidemic = no
					NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_visited_on_progress } }
				}
				preferred_limit = {
					reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -40 } 
					OR = {
						tier = KING
						AND = {
							OR = {
								tier = DUKE
								liege = { character = ROOT }
							}
							OR = {
								NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = -25 } }
								reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 40 } 
							}
						}
					}
				}
				score_value = {
					value = 1
					
					additive_modifier = {
						NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = -75 } }
						value = 0.25
					}
					additive_modifier = {
						NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = -50 } }
						value = 0.25
					}
					additive_modifier = {
						NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = -25 } }
						value = 0.25
					}
					additive_modifier = {
						NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 } }
						value = 0.25
					}
				}
				opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_visited_on_progress months = 48 }
				capital_scope = { add_province_modifier = { name = received_progress_visit_OK duration = 1825 } } 
				prestige = 50 
				wealth = -50
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_dlc = "Reapers"
					}
					custom_tooltip = {
						text = capital_prospers_custom_tooltip
						hidden_tooltip = {
							capital_scope = {
								change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = 8 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
						NOT = { is_friend = ROOT }
						NOT = { is_rival = ROOT }
						OR = {
							opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
							NOT = { age_diff = { who = ROOT years = 15 } }
						}
					}
					random = {
						chance = 4
						add_friend = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			#Random event outcomes
			random_list = { # Local nobles outcome
				90 = {
				}
				5 = {
					change_diplomacy = 1
					prestige = 15
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { trait = gregarious } 
							NOT = { trait = shy }
							NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
						}
						random = {
							chance = 25
							add_trait = gregarious
							character_event = { id = 38265 }
						}
					}
				}
				5 = {
					change_diplomacy = -1
					prestige = -15
					if = {
						limit = { 
							NOT = { trait = rude } 
							NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
						}
						random = {
							chance = 25
							add_trait = rude
							character_event = { id = trait_notification.13 }
						}
					}

		trigger = { has_character_flag = storm_injured }
		if = { 
			limit = { is_maimed_trigger = yes } 
			health = -1
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { trait = wounded } 
			hidden_tooltip = { remove_trait = wounded }
			add_maimed_trait_effect = yes 
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { trait = wounded }
				NOT = { is_maimed_trigger = yes } 
			}
			add_trait_silently_wounded_effect = yes 
		}
		clr_character_flag = storm_injured
	}
}
# Attacked by pirates/bandits
character_event = {
	id = wikid.301
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.301
		picture = GFX_evt_reaving3
		trigger = { has_character_flag = wikid_pirate_attack }
	}	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.301B
		picture = GFX_evt_bandits
		trigger = { NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_pirate_attack } }
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes 
	has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = touring_royal_progress }
					AND = {
						capital_scope = { port = yes }
						event_target:tour_destination = { port = yes }
					}	
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				set_character_flag = wikid_pirate_attack
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Fight!
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAwikid.301
			trigger = { has_character_flag = wikid_pirate_attack }
		}	
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAwikid.301B
			trigger = { NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_pirate_attack } }
		}	
		random_list = {
			70 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.66
					NOT = { combat_rating = 40 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					combat_rating = 60
				}
				set_character_flag = pirates_survive
				character_event = { id = wikid.302 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.301_survive }
			}
			25 = {
				set_character_flag = pirates_injured
				character_event = { id = wikid.302 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.301_wounded }
			}
			5 = {
				random_friend = {
					limit = { trait = dragon }
					random = {
						chance = 50
						death = { death_reason = death_missing }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { any_artifact = { has_artifact_flag = valyrian_steel } }
					set_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPwikidswordlost }
				}
				any_artifact = {
					limit = { has_artifact_flag = wikid_quest_artifact }
					unsafe_destroy_artifact = yes
				}
				death = { death_reason = death_missing }
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

	}
	
	immediate = {

			}

		}
		
		#progress outcome
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = touring_royal_progress }
			random_list = {
				5 = { 
					trigger = { diplomacy = 8 }
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						has_character_modifier = progress_entourage_huge
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						diplomacy = 12
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						diplomacy = 16
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						diplomacy = 20
					}
					set_character_flag = royal_progress_GREAT 
				}
				10 = { set_character_flag = royal_progress_OK }
				5 = { 
					trigger = { NOT = { diplomacy = 10 } }
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						NOR = {
							has_character_modifier = progress_entourage_huge
							has_character_modifier = progress_entourage_large
						}	
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						NOT = { diplomacy = 6 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						NOT = { diplomacy = 2 }
					}
					set_character_flag = royal_progress_BAD 
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # You are welcomed by the province owner
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAwikid.303
			trigger = {
				NOT = { has_character_flag = touring_royal_progress }
				event_target:tour_destination = { NOT = { has_province_flag = ruined_province } }
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAwikid.303B
			trigger = {
				event_target:tour_destination = { has_province_flag = ruined_province }
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAwikid.303C
			trigger = {
				has_character_flag = touring_royal_progress
				NOT = { event_target:tour_destination = { has_province_flag = ruined_province } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = touring_royal_progress }
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = royal_progress_GREAT  }
				event_target:tour_destination = {
					add_province_modifier = { name = received_progress_visit_GREAT duration = 1825 } 
					owner = { opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pleased months = 48 multiplier = 2 } }
				} 
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = royal_progress_OK }
				event_target:tour_destination = { add_province_modifier = { name = received_progress_visit_OK duration = 1825 } } 
			}
			if = {

				event_target:tour_destination = { 
					add_province_modifier = { name = received_progress_visit_BAD duration = 1825 }
					owner = { opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_irritated months = 48 multiplier = 2 } }
				} 
			}
		}
		event_target:tour_destination = { 
			holder_scope = { character_event = { id = wikid.304 } } #inform of arrival
		} 
	}
}
# Province owner recieves event
character_event = {
	id = wikid.304	
	picture = GFX_evt_diplomatic_greeting
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.304
		trigger = {
			FROM = { NOT = { has_character_flag = touring_royal_progress } }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.304B
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				has_character_flag = touring_royal_progress
				has_character_flag = royal_progress_GREAT 
			}	
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.304C
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				has_character_flag = touring_royal_progress
				has_character_flag = royal_progress_OK
			}	
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.304D
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				has_character_flag = touring_royal_progress
				has_character_flag = royal_progress_BAD 
			}	
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.304 
		FROM = { 
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = touring_royal_progress }
				ROOT = { 
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT_FROM = { has_character_modifier = progress_entourage_huge } }
						prestige = 100
						wealth = -100
					}	
					else_if = {
						limit = { ROOT_FROM = { has_character_modifier = progress_entourage_large } }
						prestige = 50 
						wealth = -50
					}	
					else = {
						prestige = 25 
						wealth = -25
					}	
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_character_modifier = holding_large_feast } }
						add_character_modifier = {
							name = holding_large_feast
							duration = 30
						}		
						hidden_tooltip = {	#trigger random feast events
							
							ROOT_FROM = { 
								save_event_target_as = progress_feast_target 
								character_event = { id = feast.3 }
							}
							set_character_flag = holding_progress_feast
							random = {
								chance = 7
								character_event = { id = 72004 days = 1 } #castle problems
							}
							random = {
								chance = 2
								modifier = {
									factor = 20
									capital_scope = {
										has_province_modifier = highway_robber_band
									}
								}
								character_event = { id = 72005 days = 1 } #Send Marshal to deal with Highway Robber Band
							}
							random = {
								chance = 7
								modifier = {
									factor = 2
									trait = hunter
								}
								character_event = { id = 72008 days = 1 } #Hunt for boars for winter feast
							}
							
							character_event = { id = feast.2 days = 6 }
							
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_dlc = "Reapers"
							}
							custom_tooltip = {
								text = capital_prospers_custom_tooltip
								hidden_tooltip = {
									capital_scope = {
										change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = 8 }
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}	
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_character_flag = royal_progress_GREAT }
					event_target:tour_destination = {
						tooltip = { add_province_modifier = { name = received_progress_visit_GREAT duration = 1825 } }
					} 
					clr_character_flag = royal_progress_GREAT
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_character_flag = royal_progress_OK }
					event_target:tour_destination = { 
						tooltip = { add_province_modifier = { name = received_progress_visit_OK duration = 1825 } }
					} 
					clr_character_flag = royal_progress_OK
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_character_flag = royal_progress_BAD }
					event_target:tour_destination = { 
						tooltip = { add_province_modifier = { name = received_progress_visit_BAD duration = 1825 } }
					} 
					clr_character_flag = royal_progress_BAD
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = wikid.305 } 
		}
	}
	
}
# Event selector at destination
character_event = {
	id = wikid.305
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour
	
	immediate = {
		event_target:tour_destination = { 
			owner = { save_event_target_as = tour_destination_owner } 
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour_alchemist } }
			change_variable = { which = "tour_stops" value = 1 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = { event_target:tour_destination = { province_id = 834 } } #Thousand Islands
			random = {
				chance = 50
				character_event = { id = essos.1159 days = 7 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { event_target:tour_destination = { region = world_sothoryos } } 
			random_list = {
				70 = {
				}
				20 = { #find valuable items
					set_character_flag = wikid_sothoryos_trigger
					character_event = { id = sothoryos.20 days = 7 }
				}
				5 = { #Red Death
					trigger = {
						has_epidemic = no
						NOT = { has_character_flag = immune_red_death }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.25
						resistant_to_illness_trigger = yes
					}
					character_event = { id = sothoryos.7 days = 7 }
				}
				5 = { #Misc Sothoryos Dangers

					set_character_flag = wikid_sothoryos_trigger
					character_event = { id = sothoryos.15 days = 7 }
				}			
			}	
		}

		if = {
			limit = { event_target:tour_destination = { NOT = { has_province_flag = ruined_province } } }

				20 = { # No event
				}
				10 = { # Visit a tavern and get into a brawl
					trigger = { 
						event_target:tour_destination = {
							NOT = { culture_group = ROOT }
							OR = {
								NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
								owner = { NOT = { is_liege_or_above = ROOT } }
							}	
						}
						OR = {
							is_female = no
							female_get_masculine_event_trigger = yes
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						has_character_flag = foreign_tour_brawl_event
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = drunkard
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = hedonist
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = gregarious
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.33
						trait = shy
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.33
						trait = temperate
					}
					set_character_flag = foreign_tour_brawl_event				
					character_event = { id = wikid.314 days = 2 random = 5 }
				}
				10 = { # Stumble into a brothel
					trigger = {
						NOR = { 
							trait = celibate
							trait = eunuch
						}
						OR = {
							is_female = no
							trait = homosexual
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						has_character_flag = foreign_tour_brothel_event
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = lustful
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = hedonist
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.33
						trait = honorable
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						event_target:tour_destination = { holder_scope = { has_character_modifier = owns_a_brothel } }
					}
					set_character_flag = foreign_tour_brothel_event
					character_event = { id = wikid.316 days = 2 random = 5 }
				}
				10 = { # Visit local nobles and try to make a good impression

							NOT = { culture_group = ROOT }
							OR = {
								NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }

							}	
						}
					}	
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						has_character_flag = touring_westeros
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5

				}

						has_character_flag = foreign_tour_smith

					character_event = { id = wikid.320 days = 6 }
				}
				10 = { # Walk through the streets and see peasants/slaves

				}
				10 = { # Talk with local traders
					modifier = {

				}
				10 = { # Some men wish to join you
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.1
						has_character_flag = foreign_tour_men_event
					}
					set_character_flag = foreign_tour_men_event
					character_event = { id = wikid.326 days = 2 random = 5 }
				}
				10 = { # Make a foreign lover		
					trigger = {
						NOR = { 
							trait = celibate
							trait = eunuch
							AND = {
								trait = chaste

								}
							}

					}
					modifier = {

					modifier = {

						has_lover = no
					}
					set_character_flag = foreign_tour_lover_event
					character_event = { id = wikid.328 days = 6 random = 2 }
				}
				10 = { # Make a foreign friend		
					trigger = { NOT = { num_of_friends = 4 } }
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.1
						has_character_flag = foreign_tour_friend_event
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.25
						trait = shy
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 4
						trait = gregarious
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						NOT = { num_of_friends = 1 }
					}
					set_character_flag = foreign_tour_friend_event
					character_event = { id = wikid.385 days = 6 random = 2 }
				}
				10 = { # Host persuaded to leave hostile faction	
					trigger = { 
						diplomacy = 8
						event_target:tour_destination = {
							owner = {
								liege = { character = ROOT }
								OR = {
									in_faction = yes 
									leads_faction = yes 
								} 
								NOT = { trait = incapable }
								NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_coerced_into_leaving_faction } }
								NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_refused_faction_scheme } }
								NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_delined_faction_scheme } }	
								NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_member }
								age = 16
								prisoner = no
								higher_tier_than = BARON
								NOT = { in_faction = faction_liege_loyalist }
								NOT = {
									AND = {
										liege = { tier = EMPEROR }
										in_faction = faction_crown_loyalist
									}
								}
							}	
						}	
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						diplomacy = 12
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						diplomacy = 16
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						diplomacy = 20
					}
					character_event = { id = wikid.390 days = 6 random = 2 }
				}
				10 = { # Diplomatic incident
					trigger = { 
						NOT = { diplomacy = 12 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.1
						has_character_flag = foreign_tour_bad_diplo_event
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						NOT = { diplomacy = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						NOT = { diplomacy = 4 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						NOT = { diplomacy = 1 }
					}
					set_character_flag = foreign_tour_bad_diplo_event
					character_event = { id = wikid.395 days = 6 random = 2 }
				}
				5 = { # Kidnapped by host????
					trigger = { 
						event_target:tour_destination = {
							owner = {
								NOT = { trait = honest }
								NOT = { trait = honorable }
								OR = { #Motives
									plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
									has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_vengeance }	 #Seeks vengeance
									reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_claimant_adventure_target } #Is planning adventure against me
									AND = { #Claimant
										any_demesne_title = {
											ROOT = { has_claim = PREV }
										}
										NOT = { current_heir = { character = ROOT } }
										ROOT = {
											NOT = { is_child_of = ROOT }
											NOT = { is_married = ROOT }
											NOT = { liege = { character = ROOT } }
										}			
									}
									AND = { #Dangerous Vassal
										any_vassal = { 
											character = ROOT
											OR = {
												AND = {
													relative_power_to_liege = 0.25
													NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = -50 } }
												}
												AND = {
													leads_faction = yes 
													NOT = { leads_faction = faction_liege_loyalist }
													NOT = { leads_faction = faction_crown_loyalist }
												}	
											}	
										}							
									}
									AND = { #Potential forced marriage target
										is_married = no
										is_female = no
										NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = 40 } }
										can_marry = ROOT
										ROOT = {
											is_female = yes
											age = 10
											is_married = no
											is_incapable = no
											NOT = { age = 30 }
											OR = {
												#Target has a title or claim that is equal or higher to FROM's rank
												NOT = { lower_tier_than = ROOT }
												any_heir_title = { NOT = { lower_tier_than = ROOT } }
												any_claim = { NOT = { lower_tier_than = ROOT } }
												AND = { #Horny bastard
													has_fair_trait_trigger = yes
													ROOT = { trait = lustful }
												}
											}
										}	
										NOT = { trait = celibate }
										NOT = { trait = eunuch }
									}
									# Go nuts...
									trait = lunatic
									trait = possessed									
								}
							}
						}	
					}
					event_target:tour_destination = {
						owner = {
							character_event = { id = wikid.400 days = 6 random = 2 }
						}
					}
				}
				3 = { # Entourage: make lover
					trigger = { 
						any_courtier_or_vassal = {
							ai = yes
							liege = { character = ROOT }
							NOT = { tier = KING }
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								ROOT = {
									OR = {
										has_character_modifier = progress_entourage_huge
										has_character_modifier = progress_entourage_large
									}
								}								
							}	
							is_councillor = no
							is_voter = no
							NOT = { has_minor_title = title_regent }
							in_command = no
							is_abroad = no
							NOT = { trait = slave }
							NOT = { trait = dragon }
							NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
							prisoner = no
							NOT = { trait = incapable }
							age = 16	
													
							has_lover = no
							NOR = { 
								trait = celibate
								trait = eunuch
								AND = {
									trait = chaste
									OR = {
										is_married = yes
										has_lover = yes
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						has_character_modifier = progress_entourage_huge
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						has_character_modifier = progress_entourage_large
					}
					character_event = { id = wikid.410 days = 6 random = 2 }
				}
				3 = { # Entourage: conflict
					trigger = { 
						any_courtier_or_vassal = {
							ai = yes
							liege = { character = ROOT }
							NOT = { tier = KING }
							OR = {
								is_ruler = no
								ROOT = {
									OR = {
										has_character_modifier = progress_entourage_huge
										has_character_modifier = progress_entourage_large
									}
								}								
							}	
							is_councillor = no
							is_voter = no
							NOT = { has_minor_title = title_regent }
							in_command = no
							is_abroad = no
							NOT = { trait = slave }
							NOT = { trait = dragon }
							NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
							prisoner = no
							NOT = { trait = incapable }
							age = 16	
													
							combat_rating = 20
							NOR = {
								trait = patient
								trait = craven
								trait = humble
							}
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						has_character_modifier = progress_entourage_huge
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						has_character_modifier = progress_entourage_large
					}
					character_event = { id = wikid.415 days = 6 random = 2 }
				}
			}
		}	
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = no_special_event } }
			long_character_event = { id = wikid.306 days = 5 }
		}
		else = { clr_character_flag = no_special_event }
	}
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

				}
			}
		}
		random_list = {

					factor = 0.66

				}

			}

					limit = { trait = dragon }

						chance = 50

					}
				}
				death = { death_reason = death_missing }
			}
		}
	}

							}
						}
					}

				}
			}	
		}
	}

				PREV = { liege = { move_character = PREVPREV } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { trait = deceitful } 
				NOT = { trait = honest }
				NOT = { trait = honorable }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_trait = deceitful
				character_event = { id = 38255 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

					}
				}
			}
		}

			modifier = {

						add_trait = slave

							limit = { 
								OR = {
									is_female = no 
									female_warrior_culture_trigger = yes
								}	
							}
							random_list = {
								40 = { }
								30 = { add_trait = poor_warrior }
								25 = { add_trait = trained_warrior }
								5 = { add_trait = skilled_warrior }
							}				
						}
						if = { #Invalid Kingslander
							limit = {
								226 = { NOT = { has_province_flag = kings_landing_established } }
								culture = crownlander
							}
							culture = riverlander
						}
					}
				}
			}	
		}
		wealth = -35
	}
	option = { # Ignore the commoners
		name = EVTOPTCwikid.322
		ai_chance = {

# Some men wish to join you

	id = wikid.326
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.326
	picture = GFX_evt_busy_trading_dock_republic

	has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour
	
	trigger = { ai = no }
	
	immediate = {
		event_target:tour_destination = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						female_warrior_culture_trigger = yes
					}
				}

					random_traits = yes

					religion = THIS

					historical = yes
				}
				new_character = {

						culture = PREV
						religion = PREV

						62 = { add_trait = trained_warrior }
						25 = { add_trait = skilled_warrior }
						3 = { add_trait = master_warrior }

					if = {
						limit = { religion = the_seven }
						knight_character_effect = yes
					}

					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.499 } }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					female_warrior_culture_trigger = yes
				}

					random_traits = yes
					female = yes
					culture = THIS
					religion = THIS

					historical = yes

				new_character = {

						culture = PREV
						religion = PREV
					}
					save_event_target_as = wikid.326_new_man
					random_list = {
						10 = { add_trait = poor_warrior }
						62 = { add_trait = trained_warrior }
						25 = { add_trait = skilled_warrior }
						3 = { add_trait = master_warrior }

						knight_character_effect = yes

			}
		}
	}

			}

	}

		hidden_tooltip = { event_target:wikid.326_new_man = { death = yes } }

# Make a foreign lover
character_event = {
	id = wikid.328
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.328
	picture = GFX_evt_lovers
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	portrait = event_target:foreign_lover
	
	immediate = {
		event_target:tour_destination = {
			holder_scope = {
				random_courtier = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						OR = {
							AND = {
								same_sex = ROOT
								trait = homosexual
								ROOT = { trait = homosexual }
							}
							AND = {
								NOT = { same_sex = ROOT }
								NOT = { trait = homosexual }
								ROOT = { NOT = { trait = homosexual } }
							}
							AND = {
								trait = lustful
								ROOT = { 
									trait = lustful
									culture_group = dornish
								}
							}
						}	
						is_ruler = no
						has_lover = no
						is_married = no
						is_close_relative = PREV
						liege = { character = PREVPREV }
						age = 16
						NOT = { age_diff = { who = ROOT years = 11 } }
						prisoner = no
						NOT = { trait = celibate }
						NOT = { trait = incapable }
						NOT = { trait = chaste }				
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = -20 }
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -20 }
						has_epidemic = no
						NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
						NOT_mythical_creature_trigger = yes
					}	
					save_event_target_as = foreign_lover
					break = yes
				}	
				random_courtier = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						OR = {
							AND = {
								same_sex = ROOT
								trait = homosexual
								ROOT = { trait = homosexual }
							}
							AND = {
								NOT = { same_sex = ROOT }
								NOT = { trait = homosexual }
								ROOT = { NOT = { trait = homosexual } }
							}
							AND = {
								trait = lustful
								ROOT = { 
									trait = lustful
									culture_group = dornish
								}
							}
						}	
						is_ruler = no
						has_lover = no
						is_married = no
						liege = { character = PREVPREV }
						age = 16
						NOT = { age_diff = { who = ROOT years = 11 } }
						prisoner = no
						NOT = { trait = celibate }
						NOT = { trait = incapable }
						NOT = { trait = chaste }				
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = -10 }
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -10 }
						has_epidemic = no
						NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
						NOT_mythical_creature_trigger = yes
					}	
					save_event_target_as = foreign_lover
					break = yes
				}	
				capital_scope = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							ROOT = { NOT = { prefers_men_trigger = yes } }
						}
						create_character = {
							random_traits = yes
							dynasty = none
							female = yes
							culture = THIS
							religion = PREV
							historical = yes
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							ROOT = { prefers_men_trigger = yes }
						}
						create_character = {
							random_traits = yes
							dynasty = none
							culture = THIS
							religion = PREV
							historical = yes
						}
					}
					new_character = {
						remove_trait = ugly
						random = {
							chance = 25
							add_trait = fair
						}
						remove_trait = slow
						remove_trait = imbecile
						remove_trait = dull
						remove_trait = chaste
						remove_trait = celibate
						if = {
							limit = { same_sex = ROOT }
							add_trait = homosexual
						}
						move_character = PREVPREV
						save_event_target_as = foreign_lover						
					}
				}	
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # I shall ask to meet her in my quarters
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.328
		event_target:foreign_lover = { 
			tooltip = { show_portrait = yes }
			add_lover = ROOT
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						liege = { is_close_relative = PREV }
						is_married = yes
						is_consort = yes
						is_landed = yes
						has_job_title = yes
						has_minor_title = yes
						is_voter = yes
						trait = kingsguard
						trait = nightswatch
						trait = slave
					}
				}
				move_character = ROOT
			}	
		}
		event_target:tour_destination = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = { id = wikid.329 }
			}
		}
		piety = -50
		if = {
			limit = { is_married = yes }
			piety = -100
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				trait = chaste 
				NOT = { trait = stressed }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_trait = stressed
				character_event = { id = 38282 }
			}			
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { trait = lustful }
				NOT = { trait = chaste }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_trait = lustful
				character_event = { id = 38272 }
			}
			
		}
	}
	option = { # I think not
		name = EVTOPTBwikid.328
		event_target:foreign_lover = { 
			tooltip = { show_portrait = yes }
		}	
		piety = 25

			}

		}

			}

# Offered a marriage from foreign tourist
character_event = {
	id = wikid.331
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.331
	picture = GFX_evt_emissary
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		#Determine marriage prestige
		if = {
			limit = { 
				FROM = { 
					OR = {
						father_even_if_dead = { tier = emperor } 
						mother_even_if_dead = { tier = emperor } 
					}	
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300 }
				FROM = { 
					OR = {
						father_even_if_dead = { tier = king } 
						mother_even_if_dead = { tier = king } 
					}	
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300 }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150 }
				FROM = { 
					OR = {
						father_even_if_dead = { tier = duke } 
						mother_even_if_dead = { tier = duke } 
					}	
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300 }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150 }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75 }
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Yes, let us bind our families together
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.331
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = { #Would prefer a matrilineal marriage
				factor = 0
				is_patrician = no
				event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = {
					ROOT = { current_heir = { character = PREVPREV } }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				religion_group = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = zealous
				NOT = { religion = FROM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				culture_group = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = proud
				NOT = { culture_group = FROM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				culture = eastern_valyrian
				NOT = { culture_group = FROM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				FROM = { tier = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.5
				FROM = { higher_tier_than = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 20 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 40 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 60 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 80 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 100 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -19 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -39 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -59 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -79 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -99 } }
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						is_betrothed = yes 
					}
					betrothed = {
						if = {
							limit = { is_ruler = yes }
							opinion = {
								who = PREV
								modifier = opinion_betrothal_broken
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { 
								is_ruler = no 
								liege = { is_close_relative = PREV }
							}
							liege = {
								opinion = {
									who = PREVPREV
									modifier = opinion_betrothal_broken
								}
							}	
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = {
			FROM = { set_character_flag = no_wedding_event }
			set_character_flag = no_wedding_event
			add_spouse = FROM
			clr_character_flag = no_wedding_event
			FROM = { clr_character_flag = no_wedding_event }
			
			# Stop impregnation if too young
			hidden_tooltip = {
				child_fertility_debuff = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { lower_tier_than = DUKE }
			wealth = -25
			FROM = { wealth = 25 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tier = DUKE }
			wealth = -50
			FROM = { wealth = 50 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tier = KING }
			wealth = -100
			FROM = { wealth = 100 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
			wealth = -200
			FROM = { wealth = 200 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300 }
			prestige = 300
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150 }
			prestige = 150
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75 }
			prestige = 75
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35 }
			prestige = 35
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35
		}
		FROM = { character_event = { id = wikid.332 } }
	}
	
	option = { # She will not marry some foreigner
		name = EVTOPTBwikid.331
		FROM = { character_event = { id = wikid.333 } }
		clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300
		clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150
		clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75
		clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35
	}
}
# Marriage accepted
character_event = {
	id = wikid.332
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.332
	picture = GFX_evt_marriage
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour
	
	immediate = {
		#Determine marriage prestige
		if = {
			limit = { 
				event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = { 
					OR = {
						father_even_if_dead = { tier = emperor } 
						mother_even_if_dead = { tier = emperor } 
					}	
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300 }
				event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = { 
					OR = {
						father_even_if_dead = { tier = king } 
						mother_even_if_dead = { tier = king } 
					}	
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300 }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150 }
				event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = { 
					OR = {
						father_even_if_dead = { tier = duke } 
						mother_even_if_dead = { tier = duke } 
					}	
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300 }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150 }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75 }
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35
		}
	}
	
	option = { # A wonderful day!
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.332
		tooltip = {
			event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = { add_spouse = ROOT }
			if = {
				limit = { lower_tier_than = DUKE }
				FROM = { wealth = -25 }
				wealth = 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tier = DUKE }
				FROM = { wealth = -50 }
				wealth = 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tier = king }
				FROM = { wealth = -100 }
				wealth = 100
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tier = emperor }
				FROM = { wealth = -200 }
				wealth = 200
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300 }
			prestige = 300
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150 }
			prestige = 150
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75 }
			prestige = 75
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35 }
			prestige = 35
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35
		}
	}
}

# Make a foreign friend
character_event = {
	id = wikid.385
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.385
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	portrait = event_target:foreign_friend
	
	trigger = {
		event_target:tour_destination = {
			owner = {
				any_courtier = {
					war = no
					in_command = no
					prisoner = no
					age = 16		
					is_abroad = no
					location = { province_id = event_target:tour_destination }
					NOT = { trait = slave }
					NOT = { trait = dragon }
					NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
					NOT = { is_friend = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_rival = ROOT }
					opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
					reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
					OR = {
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
						NOT = { age_diff = { who = ROOT years = 15 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}	
	}
	
	immediate = {
		event_target:tour_destination = {
			owner = {
				random_courtier = {
					limit = {
						war = no
						in_command = no
						prisoner = no
						age = 16		
						is_abroad = no
						location = { province_id = event_target:tour_destination }
						NOT = { trait = slave }
						NOT = { trait = dragon }
						NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
						NOT = { is_friend = ROOT }
						NOT = { is_rival = ROOT }
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
						OR = {
							opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
							NOT = { age_diff = { who = ROOT years = 15 } }
						}
					}	
					save_event_target_as = foreign_friend
				}		
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.385
		event_target:foreign_friend = { 
			add_friend = ROOT	
			character_event = { id = wikid.386 }
		}
	}
	option = { # I think not
		name = EVTOPTBwikid.385
	}
}

# Host persuaded to leave hostile faction
character_event = {
	id = wikid.390
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.390
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		event_target:tour_destination = {
			owner = {
				liege = { character = ROOT }
				OR = {
					in_faction = yes 
					leads_faction = yes 
				} 
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_coerced_into_leaving_faction } }
				NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_refused_faction_scheme } }
				NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_delined_faction_scheme } }	
				NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_member }
				age = 16
				prisoner = no
				higher_tier_than = BARON
				NOT = { in_faction = faction_liege_loyalist }
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						liege = { tier = EMPEROR }
						in_faction = faction_crown_loyalist
					}
				}
			}
		}	
	}
	
	immediate = {
		event_target:tour_destination = {
			owner = {
				save_event_target_as = faction_member
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.390
		tooltip_info = diplomacy
		event_target:faction_member = { 
			character_event = { id = wikid.391 tooltip =  EVTTOOLTIPwikid.391 }
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_coerced_into_leaving_faction
				who = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

# Diplomatic Incident
character_event = {
	id = wikid.395
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.395
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		event_target:tour_destination = {
			owner = {
				save_event_target_as = faction_member
			}
		}
		#find ring leader
		random_courtier_or_vassal = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				liege = { character = ROOT }
				NOT = { tier = KING }
				OR = {
					is_ruler = no
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							has_character_modifier = progress_entourage_huge
							has_character_modifier = progress_entourage_large
						}
					}								
				}	
				is_councillor = no
				is_voter = no
				NOT = { has_minor_title = title_regent }
				in_command = no
				is_abroad = no
				NOT = { trait = slave }
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
				NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				age = 16
				
				NOT = { age = 40 }			
				OR = {	
					is_female = no
					female_get_masculine_event_trigger = yes
				}
				has_severe_disability_trigger = no
				NOT = { trait = kind }
				NOT = { trait = honorable }
				NOT = { trait = just }
			}
			preferred_limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = lunatic
					trait = cruel
					trait = ruthless
					trait = arbitrary
					trait = selfish
					trait = drunkard
					trait = hedonist
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = ringleader
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.395 #Oh well
		show_portrait =  event_target:ringleader
		event_target:faction_member = { 
			character_event = { id = wikid.396 }
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_angry
				who = ROOT
				months = 36
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBwikid.395 #Buy off
		tooltip = { transfer_scaled_wealth = { from = ROOT to = event_target:faction_member value = 0.25 min = 25 max = 100 } }
		event_target:faction_member = { 		
			character_event = { id = wikid.397 tooltip =  EVTTOOLTIPwikid.397 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCwikid.395 #Use intrigue
		trigger = { intrigue = 10 }
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		prestige = -100
		event_target:faction_member = { 
			character_event = { id = wikid.398 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPwikid.398 }
		}
	}
}

# Target gets abducted... or not.
character_event = {

					is_ruler = no
					is_councillor = no
					is_voter = no

		if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = progress_entourage_large }
			any_courtier = {
				limit = {
					is_ruler = no

					is_voter = no

					NOT = { trait = slave }

				clr_character_flag = lost_trial_by_combat
				clr_character_flag = demmanded_first_trial_by_combat
				clr_character_flag = choosing_champion
				clr_character_flag = select_champion
				set_character_flag = kidnapped_by_plot

			}
		}

		clr_character_flag = lost_trial_by_combat
		clr_character_flag = demmanded_first_trial_by_combat
		clr_character_flag = choosing_champion
		clr_character_flag = select_champion
		set_character_flag = kidnapped_by_plot
		remove_trait = wikid
		character_event = { id = wikid.340 }
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			opinion = { who = FROM modifier = kidnapped_me months = 1200 }
			father = { opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_kidnapped_kin months = 600 } }
			mother = { opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_kidnapped_kin months = 600 } }
			any_sibling = { opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_kidnapped_kin months = 600 } }
			any_spouse = {
				limit = { NOT = { sibling = ROOT } }
				opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_kidnapped_kin months = 600 }
			}
			any_child = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_married = ROOT } }
				opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_kidnapped_kin months = 600 }
			}
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					is_close_relative = ROOT
					NOT = { is_parent_of = ROOT } 
					NOT = { sibling = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_married = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_child_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
				}
				opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_kidnapped_kin months = 600 }
			}
			FROM = {
				character_event = { id = wikid.402 }
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = spy_success
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPT_WOL_2121
		
		trigger = { NOT = { has_character_flag = spy_success } }
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				character_event = { id = wikid.403 }
			}
		}
	}
}

					}

			}
		}
	}

# Entourage makes a foreign lover
character_event = {
	id = wikid.410
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier_or_vassal = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				liege = { character = ROOT }
				NOT = { tier = KING }
				OR = {
					is_ruler = no
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							has_character_modifier = progress_entourage_huge
							has_character_modifier = progress_entourage_large
						}
					}								
				}	
				is_councillor = no
				is_voter = no
				NOT = { has_minor_title = title_regent }
				in_command = no
				is_abroad = no
				NOT = { trait = slave }
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
				NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				age = 16	
										
				has_lover = no
				NOT = { is_married = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_consort = ROOT }
				NOR = { 
					trait = celibate
					trait = eunuch
					AND = {
						trait = chaste
						OR = {
							is_married = yes
							has_lover = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			preferred_limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = lustful
					trait = hedonist
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = entourage_lover_maker
			ROOT = { character_event = { id = wikid.411 } }
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
# Inform
character_event = {
	id = wikid.411
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.411
	picture = GFX_evt_viking_throneroom_oldgods
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	portrait = event_target:entourage_lover_maker
	
	immediate = {
		event_target:tour_destination = {
			holder_scope = {
				random_courtier = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						OR = {
							AND = {
								same_sex = event_target:entourage_lover_maker
								trait = homosexual
								event_target:entourage_lover_maker = { trait = homosexual }
							}
							AND = {
								NOT = { same_sex = event_target:entourage_lover_maker }
								NOT = { trait = homosexual }
								event_target:entourage_lover_maker = { NOT = { trait = homosexual } }
							}
							AND = {
								trait = lustful
								event_target:entourage_lover_maker = { 
									trait = lustful
									culture_group = dornish
								}
							}
						}	
						is_ruler = no
						has_lover = no
						is_married = no				
						liege = { character = PREVPREV }
						age = 16
						NOT = { age_diff = { who = event_target:entourage_lover_maker years = 11 } }
						prisoner = no
						NOT = { trait = celibate }
						NOT = { trait = incapable }
						NOT = { trait = chaste }				
						opinion = { who = event_target:entourage_lover_maker value = -20 }
						reverse_opinion = { who = event_target:entourage_lover_maker value = -20 }
						has_epidemic = no
						NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
						NOT_mythical_creature_trigger = yes
					}	
					preferred_limit = {
						is_close_relative = PREV
						opinion = { who = event_target:entourage_lover_maker value = 10 }
						reverse_opinion = { who = event_target:entourage_lover_maker value = 10 }
					}
					preferred_limit = {
						opinion = { who = event_target:entourage_lover_maker value = 10 }
						reverse_opinion = { who = event_target:entourage_lover_maker value = 10 }
					}
					preferred_limit = {
						is_close_relative = PREV
					}
					save_event_target_as = foreign_lover
					break = yes
				}		
				capital_scope = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:entourage_lover_maker = { NOT = { prefers_men_trigger = yes } }
						}
						create_character = {
							random_traits = yes
							dynasty = none
							female = yes
							culture = THIS
							religion = PREV
							historical = yes
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:entourage_lover_maker = { prefers_men_trigger = yes }
						}
						create_character = {
							random_traits = yes
							dynasty = none
							culture = THIS
							religion = PREV
							historical = yes
						}
					}
					new_character = {
						remove_trait = ugly
						random = {
							chance = 25
							add_trait = fair
						}
						remove_trait = slow
						remove_trait = imbecile
						remove_trait = dull
						remove_trait = chaste
						remove_trait = celibate
						if = {
							limit = { same_sex = event_target:entourage_lover_maker }
							add_trait = homosexual
						}
						move_character = PREVPREV
						save_event_target_as = foreign_lover						
					}
				}	
			}
		}
	}	
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.411
		event_target:entourage_lover_maker = {
			add_lover = event_target:foreign_lover
		}
		show_portrait = event_target:foreign_lover
	}
}

# Inform
character_event = {
	id = wikid.416
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.416
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	portrait = event_target:entourage_conflict_maker
	
	immediate = {
		event_target:tour_destination = {
			owner = {
				random_courtier = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes	
						NOT = { character = PREV }
						has_lover = no
						is_married = no
						liege = { character = PREVPREV }
						age = 16
						prisoner = no
						NOT = { trait = incapable }		
						NOT = { opinion = { who = event_target:entourage_conflict_maker value = 0 } }
						NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = event_target:entourage_lover_maker value = 0 } }
						has_epidemic = no
						NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
						NOT_mythical_creature_trigger = yes
						combat_rating = 20
						NOR = {
							trait = patient
							trait = craven
							trait = humble
						}
					}	
					preferred_limit = {
						is_close_relative = PREV
						NOT = { opinion = { who = event_target:entourage_conflict_maker value = -30 } }
						NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = event_target:entourage_lover_maker value = -30 } }
					}
					preferred_limit = {
						NOT = { opinion = { who = event_target:entourage_conflict_maker value = -30 } }
						NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = event_target:entourage_lover_maker value = -30 } }
					}
					preferred_limit = {
						is_close_relative = PREV
					}
					save_event_target_as = conflict_target
					break = yes
				}		
				capital_scope = {
					create_character = {
						random_traits = yes
						dynasty = none
						female = no
						culture = THIS
						religion = PREV
						historical = yes
					}
					new_character = {				
						move_character = PREVPREV
						random_list = {
							20 = { add_trait = skilled_warrior }
							40 = { add_trait = trained_warrior }
							40 = { add_trait = poor_warrior }
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_knighthood_religion_trigger = yes }
							knight_character_effect = yes
						}
						save_event_target_as = conflict_target					
					}
				}	
			}
		}
	}	
	
	option = { #Reprimand
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.416
		prestige = -50
		event_target:entourage_conflict_maker = {
			show_scope_change = no
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_reprimanded_me months = 48 }
		}
		event_target:tour_destination = {
			show_scope_change = no
			owner = {
				show_scope_change = no
				show_portrait = THIS
				opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_satisfied months = 48 multiplier = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Back courtier
		name = EVTOPTBwikid.416
		event_target:entourage_conflict_maker = {
			show_scope_change = no
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_supported_me months = 48 }
		}
		event_target:tour_destination = {
			show_scope_change = no
			owner = {
				show_scope_change = no
				show_portrait = THIS
				opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_offended months = 48 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Use diplomacy
		name = EVTOPTCwikid.416
		trigger = { diplomacy = 10 }
		tooltip_info = diplomacy
		event_target:entourage_conflict_maker = {
			show_scope_change = no
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_supported_me months = 48 }
		}
		event_target:tour_destination = {
			show_scope_change = no
			owner = {
				show_scope_change = no
				show_portrait = THIS
				opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_satisfied months = 48 multiplier = 2 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = stressed } }
			random = {
				chance = 20
				add_trait = stressed
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = { id = 38182  }
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			prestige = -75
		}
	}
	option = { #Use intrigue to blame target
		name = EVTOPTDwikid.416
		trigger = { intrigue = 10 }
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		event_target:entourage_conflict_maker = {
			show_scope_change = no
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_supported_me months = 48 }
		}
		event_target:tour_destination = {
			show_scope_change = no
			owner = {
				show_scope_change = no
				show_portrait = THIS
				opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_satisfied months = 48 multiplier = 2 }
			}
		}
		event_target:conflict_target = {
			show_scope_change = no
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_angry months = 48 multiplier = 2 }
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		event_target:entourage_conflict_maker = {
			add_rival = event_target:conflict_target
		}
		show_portrait = event_target:conflict_target
	}
}
